#Nuxeo Training - Structure templates ######Sun Seng David TAN
###What we want to do ####At the end of the course: A BookLibrary document type - Can contain Book and BookLibrary documents
##Folders are documents
###Hierarchical Structure - Tree structure like a file system
Like file systems, a Nuxeo repository has a tree structure, with nodes and leaves 
- All "folders" are documents - With the Folderish facet  - Can define sub document types for a Folderish document.
Folderish document types define which type of document it is possible to create 
###The Folderish Facet - Content tab displayed for Folderish document.
The Nuxeo UI checks the Folderish facet to display the Content tab 
- Summary tab hidden by default ![folderish](img/folderish.png) - From Nuxeo Studio: ###Exercise BookLibrary - In Studio, create a new BookLibrary document type - Use the same icons than the Book document - Add the Folderish facet to the BookLibrary type. - Set up the BookLibrary so the user can only create documents of type Book and BookLibrary
##Structure templates
###What we want to do ####At the end of the course: A new structure for the type Domain: - Sections/Book Library - Instead of Sections/Templates/Workspaces
###Structure Template Ex: Each time you create a Domain, Templates, Sections and Workspaces nodes are created - Pre-built structures - «Per document type» basis - Defines documents generated when a document is created  - Useful to setup the default structure of your repository - Can also defines the default set of permissions - Can override the existing structure template for a doc type
###Choose the type The created structure will apply to the chosen document type ![Choose the type in Studio](img/structure-template-choose.png)
###Define a Structure Template - The structure of Domain will be overriden with this one - This structure will be used - Each time a document of type Domain will be created - At startup if the database is empty
It will actually create / of type Root, that contain a structure template that will create a document /default-domain of type Domain that will use this structure
- Existing document of type Domain will keep their old structure
